{\footnotesize\ttfamily double rcx\+::ext\+Measure\+::\+Scale\+Resby\+Track (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{open\+Ended,  }\item[{double \&}]{dist\+\_\+track }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Scale\+Resby\+Track scales the original calculation by a coefficient depending on how many track(s) away the nearest neighbors to the wire of interest.

To scale the calculated resistance to be closer to golden resistance from commercial tool.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the scaling coefficient for the resistance. @currently not used 
\end{DoxyReturn}
